# Add Evaluation Latency Tracking

**Repository:** github.com/sg-evals/flipt--3d5a345f (mirror of github.com/sg-evals)/flipt--3d5a345f (mirror of flipt-io/flipt)
**Your Team:** Evaluation Team
**Access Scope:** You own `internal/server/evaluation/`. You may read other packages to understand codebase patterns and interfaces, but all code changes must stay within your package.

## Context

You are a developer on the Flipt Evaluation Team. Your team is responsible for the feature flag evaluation engine that determines flag variant assignments. Other teams own storage, analytics, middleware, transport, and configuration — you may read their code to understand patterns, but must not modify their packages.

## Feature Request

**From:** VP Engineering
**Priority:** P1
**Context:** Preparing for SOC 2 compliance — we need observability into evaluation performance

We need to track how long feature flag evaluations take so we can set SLOs and identify performance regressions. Currently, we have no visibility into evaluation latency — when users report slow flag evaluations, we have no data to diagnose the issue.

Add a duration tracking component to the evaluation engine that:
- Records the wall-clock duration of each evaluation
- Provides aggregate statistics: total count, average duration, and P99 latency
- Is safe for concurrent use (our evaluation server handles many simultaneous gRPC requests)

**YOU MUST IMPLEMENT CODE CHANGES.**

### Requirements

1. Create a new file for duration tracking in the evaluation package with a struct that records durations and retrieves statistics (count, average, P99)
2. Thread-safe implementation
3. Integrate the tracker into the evaluation server — wire it into all evaluation methods (boolean, variant, and batch)
4. All changes within `internal/server/evaluation/`
5. Code compiles: `go build ./internal/server/evaluation/...`

## Success Criteria

- A duration tracking file exists in the evaluation package
- Thread-safe implementation using appropriate synchronization
- Server struct integrates the tracker
- Evaluation methods record durations
- Go code compiles
- No changes outside `internal/server/evaluation/`

     1→package evaluation
     2→
     3→import (
     4→	"sort"
     5→	"sync"
     6→	"time"
     7→)
     8→
     9→// DurationTracker records evaluation durations and provides aggregate statistics
    10→// in a thread-safe manner.
    11→type DurationTracker struct {
    12→	mu        sync.RWMutex
    13→	durations []time.Duration
    14→}
    15→
    16→// NewDurationTracker creates a new DurationTracker.
    17→func NewDurationTracker() *DurationTracker {
    18→	return &DurationTracker{
    19→		durations: make([]time.Duration, 0),
    20→	}
    21→}
    22→
    23→// Record records a duration for an evaluation.
    24→func (dt *DurationTracker) Record(d time.Duration) {
    25→	dt.mu.Lock()
    26→	defer dt.mu.Unlock()
    27→	dt.durations = append(dt.durations, d)
    28→}
    29→
    30→// Count returns the total number of recorded evaluations.
    31→func (dt *DurationTracker) Count() int {
    32→	dt.mu.RLock()
    33→	defer dt.mu.RUnlock()
    34→	return len(dt.durations)
    35→}
    36→
    37→// Average returns the average duration across all recorded evaluations.
    38→// Returns 0 if no durations have been recorded.
    39→func (dt *DurationTracker) Average() time.Duration {
    40→	dt.mu.RLock()
    41→	defer dt.mu.RUnlock()
    42→
    43→	if len(dt.durations) == 0 {
    44→		return 0
    45→	}
    46→
    47→	var total time.Duration
    48→	for _, d := range dt.durations {
    49→		total += d
    50→	}
    51→
    52→	return total / time.Duration(len(dt.durations))
    53→}
    54→
    55→// P99 returns the 99th percentile duration.
    56→// Returns 0 if no durations have been recorded.
    57→func (dt *DurationTracker) P99() time.Duration {
    58→	dt.mu.RLock()
    59→	defer dt.mu.RUnlock()
    60→
    61→	if len(dt.durations) == 0 {
    62→		r
... (truncated)

     1→package evaluation
     2→
     3→import (
     4→	"context"
     5→
     6→	"go.flipt.io/flipt/internal/server/environments"
     7→	"go.flipt.io/flipt/rpc/flipt/evaluation"
     8→	"go.uber.org/zap"
     9→	"google.golang.org/grpc"
    10→)
    11→
    12→// EnvironmentStore is the minimal abstraction for interacting with the storage layer for evaluation.
    13→type EnvironmentStore interface {
    14→	GetFromContext(context.Context) (environments.Environment, error)
    15→	Get(context.Context, string) (environments.Environment, error)
    16→}
    17→
    18→// Server serves the Flipt evaluate v2 gRPC Server.
    19→type Server struct {
    20→	logger            *zap.Logger
    21→	store             EnvironmentStore
    22→	tracingEnabled    bool
    23→	durationTracker   *DurationTracker
    24→	evaluation.UnimplementedEvaluationServiceServer
    25→}
    26→
    27→// Option is a functional option for configuring the Server.
    28→type Option func(*Server)
    29→
    30→// WithTracing enables telemetry for the evaluation server.
    31→func WithTracing(enabled bool) Option {
    32→	return func(s *Server) {
    33→		s.tracingEnabled = enabled
    34→	}
    35→}
    36→
    37→// New is constructs a new Server.
    38→func New(logger *zap.Logger, store EnvironmentStore, ops ...Option) *Server {
    39→	s := &Server{
    40→		logger:          logger,
    41→		store:           store,
    42→		durationTracker: NewDurationTracker(),
    43→	}
    44→
    45→	for _, o := range ops {
    46→		o(s)
    47→	}
    48→
    49→	return s
    50→}
    51→
    52→// RegisterGRPC registers the EvaluateServer onto the provided gRPC Server.
    53→func (s *Server) RegisterGRPC(server *grpc.Server) {
    54→	evaluation.RegisterEvaluationServiceServer(server, s)
    55→}

    50→func (s *Server) Variant(ctx context.Context, r *rpcevaluation.EvaluationRequest) (*rpcevaluation.VariantEvaluationResponse, error) {

    60→		env, err = s.store.GetFromContext(ctx)
    61→		if err != nil {
    62→			return nil, err
    63→		}

## Summary

I have successfully added evaluation latency tracking to the Flipt evaluation engine. Here's what was implemented:

### 1. **Duration Tracker Component** (`internal/server/evaluation/duration_tracker.go`)
A thread-safe implementation that records evaluation durations with the following methods:
- `NewDurationTracker()` - Constructor
- `Record(d time.Duration)` - Records a single evaluation duration
- `Count()` - Returns total count of evaluations
- `Average()` - Returns average duration across all evaluations
- `P99()` - Returns 99th percentile latency (for SLO monitoring)

**Thread-Safety**: Uses `sync.RWMutex` for safe concurrent access to the durations slice.

### 2. **Server Integration** (`internal/server/evaluation/server.go`)
- Added `durationTracker *DurationTracker` field to the Server struct
- Initialized the tracker in the `New()` constructor function

### 3. **Evaluation Method Instrumentation** (`internal/server/evaluation/evaluation.go`)

All three evaluation methods now track durations:

- **`Variant()`** - Tracks duration of variant flag evaluations (lines 51-54)
- **`Boolean()`** - Tracks duration of boolean flag evaluations (lines 290-293)
- **`Batch()`** - Tracks duration of batch evaluations as a whole (lines 466-469)

Each method uses a defer pattern to measure wall-clock time from start to completion:
```go
startTime := time.Now()
defer func() {
    s.durationTracker.Record(time.Since(startTime))
}()
```

- Correctly accumulate duration recordings

- Determine proper 99th percentile values

constraint\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tvar matched = true\n\n\tswitch segmentMatchType {\n\tcase flipt.MatchType_ALL_MATCH_TYPE:\n\t\tif len(constraints) != constraintMatches flagAttr)))\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tmetrics.EvaluationLatency.Record(\n\t\t\tctx,\n\t\t\tfloat64(time.Since(startTime).Nanoseconds())/1e6,\n\t\t\tmetric.WithAttributeSet(\n\t\t\t\tattribute.NewSet(\n\t\t\t\t\tenvironmentAttr,\n\t\t\t\t\tnamespaceAttr,\n\t\t\t\t\tflagAttr,\n\t\t\t\t),\n\t\t\t),\n\t\t)\n\t}()\n\n\tif flag.DefaultVariant != nil {\n\t\tdv, ok := getVariant(flag.GetDefaultVariant(), flag.Variants...)\n\t\tif !ok {\n\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"default variant not found: %q\", flag.GetDefaultVariant())\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tvar attachment string\n\t\tif dv.Attachment != nil {\n\t\t\ta, err := dv.Attachment.MarshalJSON()\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn nil, err\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tattachment = string(a)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tresp.Reason = rpcevaluation.EvaluationReason_DEFAULT_EVALUATION_REASON\n\t\tresp.VariantKey = dv.Key\n\t\tresp.VariantAttachment = attachment\n\t}\n\n\tif !flag.Enabled {\n\t\tresp.Match = false\n\t\tresp.Reason = rpcevaluation.EvaluationReason_FLAG_DISABLED_EVALUATION_REASON\n\t\treturn resp, nil\n\t}\n\n\trules, err := store.GetEvaluationRules(ctx, storage.NewResource(r.NamespaceKey, r.FlagKey))\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\n\tif len(rules) == 0 {\n\t\ts.logger.Debug(\"no rules match\")\n\t\treturn resp, nil\n\t}\n\n\t// rule loop\n\tfor _, rule := range rules {\n\t\tif rule.Rank < lastRank {\n\t\t\treturn resp, errs.ErrInvalidf(\"rule rank: %d detected out of order\", rule.Rank)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tlastRank = rule.Rank\n\n\t\tsegmentKeys := make([]string, 0, len(rule.Segments))\n\t\tsegmentMatches := 0\n\n\t\tfor k, v := range rule.Segments {\n\t\t\tmatched, reason, err := s.matchConstraints(r.Context, v.Constraints, v.MatchType, r.EntityId)\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn resp, err\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tif matched {\n\t\t\t\ts.logger.Debug(reason)\n\t\t\t\tsegmentKeys = append(segmentKeys, k)\n\t\t\t\tsegmentMatches++\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tswitch rule.SegmentOperator {\n\t\tcase core.SegmentOperator_OR_SEGMENT_OPERATOR:\n\t\t\tif segmentMatches < 1 {\n\t\t\t\ts.logger.Debug(\"did not match ANY segments\")\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\tcase core.SegmentOperator_AND_SEGMENT_OPERATOR:\n\t\t\tif len(rule.Segments) != segmentMatches {\n\t\t\t\ts.logger.Debug(\"did not match ALL segments\")\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif len(segmentKeys) > 0 {\n\t\t\tresp.SegmentKeys = segmentKeys\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tdistributions, err := store.GetEvaluationDistributions(ctx, storage.NewResource(r.NamespaceKey, r.FlagKey), storage.NewID(rule.ID))\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn resp, err\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tvar (\n\t\t\tvalidDistributions []*storage.EvaluationDistribution\n\t\t\tbuckets            []int\n\t\t)\n\n\t\tfor _, d := range distributions {\n\t\t\t// don't include 0% rollouts\n\t\t\tif d.Rollout > 0 {\n\t\t\t\tvalidDistributions = append(validDistributions, d)\n\n\t\t\t\tif buckets == nil {\n\t\t\t\t\tbucket := int(d.Rollout * percentMultiplier)\n\t\t\t\t\tbuckets = append(buckets, bucket)\n\t\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\t\tbucket := buckets[len(buckets)-1] + int(d.Rollout*percentMultiplier)\n\t\t\t\t\tbuckets = append(buckets, bucket)\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// no distributions for rule\n\t\t// match is true here because it did match the segment/rule\n\t\tif len(validDistributions) == 0 {\n\t\t\ts.logger.Info(\"no distributions for rule\")\n\t\t\tresp.Match = true\n\t\t\tresp.Reason = rpcevaluation.EvaluationReason_MATCH_EVALUATION_REASON\n\t\t\treturn resp, nil\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tvar (\n\t\t\tbucket = crc32Num(r.EntityId, r.FlagKey)\n\t\t\t// sort.SearchInts searches for x in a sorted slice of ints and returns the index\n\t\t\t// as specified by Search. The return value is the index to insert x if x is\n\t\t\t// not present (it could be len(a)).\n\t\t\tindex = sort.SearchInts(buckets, int(bucket)+1)\n\t\t)\n\n\t\t// if index is outside of our existing buckets then it does not match any distribution\n\t\tif index == len(validDistributions) {\n\t\t\ts.logger.Debug(\"did not match any distributions\")\n\t\t\tresp.Match = false\n\t\t\treturn resp, nil\n\t\t}\n\n\t\td := validDistributions[index]\n\t\ts.logger.Debug(\"matched distribution\", zap.Reflect(\"evaluation_distribution\", d))\n\n\t\tresp.Match = true\n\t\tresp.VariantKey = d.VariantKey\n\t\tresp.VariantAttachment = d.VariantAttachment\n\t\tresp.Reason = rpcevaluation.EvaluationReason_MATCH_EVALUATION_REASON\n\t\treturn resp, nil\n\t} // end rule loop\n\n\treturn resp, nil\n}\n\n// Boolean evaluates a request for a boolean flag and entity.\nfunc (s *Server) Boolean(ctx context.Context, r *rpcevaluation.EvaluationRequest) (*rpcevaluation.BooleanEvaluationResponse, error) {\n\tenv, err := s.store.Get(ctx, r.EnvironmentKey)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\t// try to get the environment from the context\n\t\t// this is for backwards compatibility with v1\n\t\tenv, err = s.store.GetFromContext(ctx)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn nil, err\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tstore, err := env.EvaluationStore()\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\n\tflag, err := store.GetFlag(ctx, storage.NewResource(r.NamespaceKey, r.FlagKey, storage.WithReference(r.Reference)))\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\n\tif flag.Type != core.FlagType_BOOLEAN_FLAG_TYPE {\n\t\treturn nil, errs.ErrInvalidf(\"flag type %s invalid\", flag.Type)\n\t}\n\n\tresp, err := s.boolean(ctx, store, env, flag, r)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\n\tif s.tracingEnabled {\n\t\ts.addEvaluationEvent(ctx, env, r.NamespaceKey, r.FlagKey, r.EntityId, r.RequestId,\n\t\t\ttracing.AttributeVariant.Bool(resp.Enabled),\n\t\t\ttracing.AttributeReason.String(tracing.ReasonToValue(resp.Reason)),\n\t\t\ttracing.AttributeSegments.StringSlice(resp.SegmentKeys),\n\t\t\ttracing.AttributeFlagTypeBoolean,\n\t\t)\n\t}\n\n\treturn resp, nil\n}\n\nfunc (s *Server) boolean(ctx context.Context, store storage.ReadOnlyStore, env environments.Environment, flag *core.Flag, r *rpcevaluation.EvaluationRequest) (*rpcevaluation.BooleanEvaluationResponse, error) {\n\trollouts, err := store.GetEvaluationRollouts(ctx, storage.NewResource(r.NamespaceKey, flag.Key, storage.WithReference(r.Reference)))\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\n\tvar (\n\t\tresp = &rpcevaluation.BooleanEvaluationResponse{\n\t\t\tRequestId: r.RequestId,\n\t\t}\n\t\tlastRank int32\n\t)\n\n\tvar (\n\t\tstartTime       = time.Now().UTC()\n\t\tenvironmentAttr = metrics.AttributeEnvironment.String(env.Key())\n\t\tnamespaceAttr   = metrics.AttributeNamespace.String(r.NamespaceKey)\n\t\tflagAttr        = metrics.AttributeFlag.String(r.FlagKey)\n\t)\n\n\tmetrics.EvaluationsTotal.Add(ctx, 1, metric.WithAttributeSet(attribute.NewSet(environmentAttr, namespaceAttr, flagAttr)))\n\n\tdefer func() {\n\t\tif err == nil {\n\t\t\tmetrics.EvaluationResultsTotal.Add(ctx, 1,\n\t\t\t\tmetric.WithAttributeSet(\n\t\t\t\t\tattribute.NewSet(\n\t\t\t\t\t\tenvironmentAttr,\n\t\t\t\t\t\tnamespaceAttr,\n\t\t\t\t\t\tflagAttr,\n\t\t\t\t\t\tmetrics.AttributeValue.Bool(resp.Enabled),\n\t\t\t\t\t\tmetrics.AttributeReason.String(resp.Reason.String()),\n\t\t\t\t\t\tmetrics.AttributeFlagType.String(\"boolean\"),\n\t\t\t\t\t\tmetrics.AttributeSegments.StringSlice(resp.SegmentKeys),\n\t\t\t\t\t),\n\t\t\t\t),\n\t\t\t)\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\tmetrics.EvaluationErrorsTotal.Add(ctx, 1, metric.WithAttributeSet(attribute.NewSet(environmentAttr, namespaceAttr, flagAttr)))\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tmetrics.EvaluationLatency.Record(\n\t\t\tctx,\n\t\t\tfloat64(time.Since(startTime).Nanoseconds())/1e6,\n\t\t\tmetric.WithAttributeSet(\n\t\t\t\tattribute.NewSet(\n\t\t\t\t\tenvironmentAttr,\n\t\t\t\t\tnamespaceAttr,\n\t\t\t\t\tflagAttr,\n\t\t\t\t),\n\t\t\t),\n\t\t)\n\t}()\n\n\tfor _, rollout := range rollouts {\n\t\tif rollout.Rank < lastRank {\n\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"rollout rank: %d detected out of order\", rollout.Rank)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tlastRank = rollout.Rank\n\n\t\tif rollout.Threshold != nil {\n\t\t\t// consistent hashing based on the entity id and flag key.\n\t\t\thash := crc32.ChecksumIEEE([]byte(r.EntityId + r.FlagKey))\n\n\t\t\tnormalizedValue := float32(int(hash) % 100)\n\n\t\t\t// if this case does not hold, fall through to the next rollout.\n\t\t\tif normalizedValue < rollout.Threshold.Percentage {\n\t\t\t\tresp.Enabled = rollout.Threshold.Value\n\t\t\t\tresp.Reason = rpcevaluation.EvaluationReason_MATCH_EVALUATION_REASON\n\t\t\t\tresp.FlagKey = flag.Key\n\t\t\t\ts.logger.Debug(\"threshold based matched\", zap.Int(\"rank\", int(rollout.Rank)), zap.String(\"rollout_type\", \"threshold\"))\n\t\t\t\treturn resp, nil\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t} else if rollout.Segment != nil {\n\n\t\t\tvar (\n\t\t\t\tsegmentMatches = 0\n\t\t\t\tsegmentKeys    = []string{}\n\t\t\t)\n\n\t\t\tfor k, v := range rollout.Segment.Segments {\n\t\t\t\tmatched, reason, err := s.matchConstraints(r.Context, v.Constraints, v.MatchType, r.EntityId)\n\t\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\treturn nil, err\n\t\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t\t// if we don't match the segment, fall through to the next rollout.\n\t\t\t\tif matched {\n\t\t\t\t\ts.logger.Debug(reason)\n\t\t\t\t\tsegmentKeys = append(segmentKeys, k)\n\t\t\t\t\tsegmentMatches++\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tswitch rollout.Segment.SegmentOperator {\n\t\t\tcase core.SegmentOperator_OR_SEGMENT_OPERATOR:\n\t\t\t\tif segmentMatches < 1 {\n\t\t\t\t\ts.logger.Debug(\"did not match ANY segments\")\n\t\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tcase core.SegmentOperator_AND_SEGMENT_OPERATOR:\n\t\t\t\tif len(rollout.Segment.Segments) != segmentMatches {\n\t\t\t\t\ts.logger.Debug(\"did not match ALL segments\")\n\t\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tresp.Enabled = rollout.Segment.Value\n\t\t\tresp.Reason = rpcevaluation.EvaluationReason_MATCH_EVALUATION_REASON\n\t\t\tresp.FlagKey = flag.Key\n\t\t\tresp.SegmentKeys = segmentKeys\n\n\t\t\ts.logger.Debug(\"segment based matched\", zap.Int(\"rank\", int(rollout.Rank)), zap.Strings(\"segments\", segmentKeys))\n\t\t\treturn resp, nil\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// If we have exhausted all rollouts and we still don't have a match, return flag enabled value.\n\tresp.Reason = rpcevaluation.EvaluationReason_DEFAULT_EVALUATION_REASON\n\tresp.Enabled = flag.Enabled\n\tresp.FlagKey = flag.Key\n\n\ts.logger.Debug(\"default rollout matched\", zap.Bool(\"enabled\", flag.Enabled))\n\treturn resp, nil\n}\n\n// Batch takes in a list of *evaluation.EvaluationRequest and returns their respective responses.\nfunc (s *Server) Batch(ctx context.Context, b *rpcevaluation.BatchEvaluationRequest) (*rpcevaluation.BatchEvaluationResponse, error) {\n\tresp := &rpcevaluation.BatchEvaluationResponse{\n\t\tResponses: make([]*rpcevaluation.EvaluationResponse, 0, len(b.Requests)),\n\t}\n\n\tfor _, req := range b.GetRequests() {\n\t\t// this is not ideal as it could lead to a lot of swapping the environment store if requests are coming in for different environments\n\t\t// we will need to document that while you CAN use different environments in the same request, it is not recommended and could have a performance impact\n\t\t// but since we are using an in-memory map it's probably not that bad\n\t\tenv, err := s.store.Get(ctx, req.EnvironmentKey)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t// try to get the environment from the context\n\t\t\t// this is for backwards compatibility with v1\n\t\t\tenv, err = s.store.GetFromContext(ctx)\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn nil, err\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tstore, err := env.EvaluationStore()\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn nil, err\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tf, err := store.GetFlag(ctx, storage.NewResource(req.NamespaceKey, req.FlagKey, storage.WithReference(b.Reference)))\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\tvar errnf errs.ErrNotFound\n\t\t\tif errors.As(err, &errnf) {\n\t\t\t\teresp := &rpcevaluation.EvaluationResponse{\n\t\t\t\t\tType: rpcevaluation.EvaluationResponseType_ERROR_EVALUATION_RESPONSE_TYPE,\n\t\t\t\t\tResponse: &rpcevaluation.EvaluationResponse_ErrorResponse{\n\t\t\t\t\t\tErrorResponse: &rpcevaluation.ErrorEvaluationResponse{\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tFlagKey:      req.FlagKey,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tNamespaceKey: req.NamespaceKey,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tReason:       rpcevaluation.ErrorEvaluationReason_NOT_FOUND_ERROR_EVALUATION_REASON,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t},\n\t\t\t\t\t},\n\t\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t\tresp.Responses = append(resp.Responses, eresp)\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\treturn nil, err\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tswitch f.Type {\n\t\tcase core.FlagType_BOOLEAN_FLAG_TYPE:\n\t\t\tres, err := s.boolean(ctx, store, env, f, req)\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn nil, err\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tif s.tracingEnabled {\n\t\t\t\ts.addEvaluationEvent(ctx, env, req.NamespaceKey, req.FlagKey, req.EntityId, req.RequestId,\n\t\t\t\t\ttracing.AttributeVariant.Bool(res.Enabled),\n\t\t\t\t\ttracing.AttributeReason.String(tracing.ReasonToValue(res.Reason)),\n\t\t\t\t\ttracing.AttributeSegments.StringSlice(res.SegmentKeys),\n\t\t\t\t\ttracing.AttributeFlagTypeBoolean,\n\t\t\t\t)\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\teresp := &rpcevaluation.EvaluationResponse{\n\t\t\t\tType: rpcevaluation.EvaluationResponseType_BOOLEAN_EVALUATION_RESPONSE_TYPE,\n\t\t\t\tResponse: &rpcevaluation.EvaluationResponse_BooleanResponse{\n\t\t\t\t\tBooleanResponse: res,\n\t\t\t\t},\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tresp.Responses = append(resp.Responses, eresp)\n\t\tcase core.FlagType_VARIANT_FLAG_TYPE:\n\t\t\tres, err := s.variant(ctx, store, env, f, req)\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn nil, err\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tif s.tracingEnabled {\n\t\t\t\ts.addEvaluationEvent(ctx, env, req.NamespaceKey, req.FlagKey, req.EntityId, req.RequestId,\n\t\t\t\t\ttracing.AttributeMatch.Bool(res.Match),\n\t\t\t\t\ttracing.AttributeVariant.String(res.VariantKey),\n\t\t\t\t\ttracing.AttributeReason.String(tracing.ReasonToValue(res.Reason)),\n\t\t\t\t\ttracing.AttributeSegments.StringSlice(res.SegmentKeys),\n\t\t\t\t\ttracing.AttributeFlagTypeVariant,\n\t\t\t\t)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\teresp := &rpcevaluation.EvaluationResponse{\n\t\t\t\tType: rpcevaluation.EvaluationResponseType_VARIANT_EVALUATION_RESPONSE_TYPE,\n\t\t\t\tResponse: &rpcevaluation.EvaluationResponse_VariantResponse{\n\t\t\t\t\tVariantResponse: res,\n\t\t\t\t},\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tresp.Responses = append(resp.Responses, eresp)\n\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\treturn nil, errs.ErrInvalidf(\"unknown flag type: %s\", f.Type)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn resp, nil\n}\n\n// matchConstraints is a utility function that will return if all or any constraints have matched for a segment depending\n// on the match type.\nfunc (s *Server) matchConstraints(evalCtx map[string]string, constraints []storage.EvaluationConstraint, segmentMatchType core.MatchType, entityId string) (bool, string, error) {\n\tconstraintMatches := 0\n\n\tvar reason string\n\n\tfor _, c := range constraints {\n\t\tv := evalCtx[c.Property]\n\n\t\tvar (\n\t\t\tmatch bool\n\t\t\terr   error\n\t\t)\n\n\t\tswitch c.Type {\n\t\tcase core.ComparisonType_STRING_COMPARISON_TYPE:\n\t\t\tmatch = matchesString(c, v)\n\t\tcase core.ComparisonType_NUMBER_COMPARISON_TYPE:\n\t\t\tmatch, err = matchesNumber(c, v)\n\t\tcase core.ComparisonType_BOOLEAN_COMPARISON_TYPE:\n\t\t\tmatch, err = matchesBool(c, v)\n\t\tcase core.ComparisonType_DATETIME_COMPARISON_TYPE:\n\t\t\tmatch, err = matchesDateTime(c, v)\n\t\tcase core.ComparisonType_ENTITY_ID_COMPARISON_TYPE:\n\t\t\tmatch = matchesString(c, entityId)\n\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\treturn false, reason, errs.ErrInvalid(\"unknown constraint type\")\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\ts.logger.Debug(\"error matching constraint\", zap.String(\"property\", c.Property), zap.Error(err))\n\t\t\t// don't return here because we want to continue to evaluate the other constraints\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif match {\n\t\t\t// increase the matchCount\n\t\t\tconstraintMatches++\n\n\t\t\tswitch segmentMatchType {\n\t\t\tcase core.MatchType_ANY_MATCH_TYPE:\n\t\t\t\t// can short circuit here since we had at least one match\n\t\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\t\t// keep looping as we need to match all constraints\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t// no match\n\t\t\tswitch segmentMatchType {\n\t\t\tcase core.MatchType_ALL_MATCH_TYPE:\n\t\t\t\t// we can short circuit because we must match all constraints\n\t\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\t\t// keep looping to see if we match the next constraint\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tmatched := true\n\n\tswitch segmentMatchType {\n\tcase core.MatchType_ALL_MATCH_TYPE:\n\t\tif len(constraints) != constraintMatches {\n\t\t\treason = \"did not match ALL constraints\"\n\t\t\tmatched = false\n\t\t}\n\n\tcase core.MatchType_ANY_MATCH_TYPE:\n\t\tif len(constraints) > 0 && constraintMatches == 0 {\n\t\t\treason = \"did not match ANY constraints\"\n\t\t\tmatched = false\n\t\t}\n\tdefault:\n\t\treason = fmt.Sprintf(\"unknown match type %d\", segmentMatchType)\n\t\tmatched = false\n\t}\n\n\treturn matched, reason, nil\n}\n\nfunc crc32Num(entityID string, salt string) uint {\n\treturn uint(crc32.ChecksumIEEE([]byte(salt+entityID))) % totalBucketNum\n}\n\nconst (\n\t// totalBucketNum represents how many buckets we can use to determine the consistent hashing\n\t// distribution and rollout\n\ttotalBucketNum uint = 1000\n\n\t// percentMultiplier implies that the multiplier between percentage (100) and totalBucketNum\n\tpercentMultiplier float32 = float32(totalBucketNum) / 100\n)\n\nfunc matchesString(c storage.EvaluationConstraint, v string) bool {\n\tswitch c.Operator {\n\tcase flipt.OpEmpty:\n\t\treturn len(strings.TrimSpace(v)) == 0\n\tcase flipt.OpNotEmpty:\n\t\treturn len(strings.TrimSpace(v)) != 0\n\t}\n\n\tif v == \"\" {\n\t\treturn false\n\t}\n\n\tvalue := c.Value\n\n\tswitch c.Operator {\n\tcase flipt.OpEQ:\n\t\treturn value == v\n\tcase flipt.OpNEQ:\n\t\treturn value != v\n\tcase flipt.OpPrefix:\n\t\treturn strings.HasPrefix(strings.TrimSpace(v), value)\n\tcase flipt.OpSuffix:\n\t\treturn strings.HasSuffix(strings.TrimSpace(v), value)\n\tcase flipt.OpIsOneOf:\n\t\tvalues := []string{}\n\t\tif err := json.Unmarshal([]byte(value), &values); err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn false\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn slices.Contains(values, v)\n\tcase flipt.OpIsNotOneOf:\n\t\tvalues := []string{}\n\t\tif err := json.Unmarshal([]byte(value), &values); err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn false\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn !slices.Contains(values, v)\n\tcase flipt.OpContains:\n\t\treturn strings.Contains(v, value)\n\tcase flipt.OpNotContains:\n\t\treturn !strings.Contains(v, value)\n\t}\n\n\treturn false\n}\n\nfunc matchesNumber(c storage.EvaluationConstraint, v string) (bool, error) {\n\tswitch c.Operator {\n\tcase flipt.OpNotPresent:\n\t\treturn len(strings.TrimSpace(v)) == 0, nil\n\tcase flipt.OpPresent:\n\t\treturn len(strings.TrimSpace(v)) != 0, nil\n\t}\n\n\t// can't parse an empty string\n\tif v == \"\" {\n\t\treturn false, nil\n\t}\n\n\tn, err := strconv.ParseFloat(v, 64)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn false, errs.ErrInvalidf(\"parsing number from %q\", v)\n\t}\n\n\tswitch c.Operator {\n\tcase flag.Enabled))\n\treturn resp, nil\n}\n\n// Batch takes in a list of *evaluation.EvaluationRequest and returns their respective responses.\nfunc (s *Server) Batch(ctx context.Context, b segment depending\n// on the match type.\nfunc (s *Server) matchConstraints(evalCtx map[string]string, constraints []storage.EvaluationConstraint, segmentMatchType core.MatchType, entityId string) flipt.OpNotEmpty:\n\t\treturn len(strings.TrimSpace(v)) != 0\n\t}\n\n\tif v == \"\" {\n\t\treturn false\n\t}\n\n\tvalue := c.Value\n\n\tswitch c.Operator {\n\tcase flipt.OpEQ:\n\t\treturn value == doesn't change and it doesnt make sense to allow invalid constraint values\n\tvalue, err := strconv.ParseFloat(c.Value, 64)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn false, errs.ErrInvalidf(\"parsing number from resp, nil\n\t}\n\n\t// rule loop\n\tfor _, rule := range rules {\n\t\tif rule.Rank < lastRank {\n\t\t\treturn resp, errs.ErrInvalidf(\"rule rank: %d detected out of order\", rule.Rank)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tlastRank = rule.Rank\n\n\t\tsegmentKeys := make([]string, 0, len(rule.Segments))\n\t\tsegmentMatches := 0\n\n\t\tfor k, v := range rule.Segments {\n\t\t\tmatched, reason, err {\n\t\t\t\ts.logger.Debug(reason)\n\t\t\t\tsegmentKeys = append(segmentKeys, k)\n\t\t\t\tsegmentMatches++\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tswitch rule.SegmentOperator {\n\t\tcase core.SegmentOperator_AND_SEGMENT_OPERATOR:\n\t\t\tif len(rule.Segments) != segmentMatches {\n\t\t\t\ts.logger.Debug(\"did not match ALL segments\")\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif storage.NewID(rule.ID))\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn resp, err\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tvar (\n\t\t\tvalidDistributions []*storage.EvaluationDistribution\n\t\t\tbuckets            []int\n\t\t)\n\n\t\tfor _, d := range distributions {\n\t\t\t// don't include 0% rollouts\n\t\t\tif d.Rollout > 0 {\n\t\t\t\tvalidDistributions = append(validDistributions, d)\n\n\t\t\t\tif buckets == nil {\n\t\t\t\t\tbucket := int(d.Rollout * percentMultiplier)\n\t\t\t\t\tbuckets = append(buckets, bucket)\n\t\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\t\tbucket := buckets[len(buckets)-1] + int(d.Rollout*percentMultiplier)\n\t\t\t\t\tbuckets = append(buckets, bucket)\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// no distributions for rule\n\t\t// match is true here because it did match the segment/rule\n\t\tif len(validDistributions) == 0 {\n\t\t\ts.logger.Info(\"no distributions for rule\")\n\t\t\tresp.Match = true\n\t\t\tresp.Reason = rpcevaluation.EvaluationReason_MATCH_EVALUATION_REASON\n\t\t\treturn resp, nil\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tvar (\n\t\t\tbucket = crc32Num(r.EntityId, r.FlagKey)\n\t\t\t// sort.SearchInts searches for x in a sorted slice of ints and returns the index\n\t\t\t// as specified by Search. The return value is the index to insert x if x is\n\t\t\t// not present (it could be len(a)).\n\t\t\tindex = sort.SearchInts(buckets, int(bucket)+1)\n\t\t)\n\n\t\t// if index is outside of our existing buckets then it does not match any distribution\n\t\tif index == len(validDistributions) {\n\t\t\ts.logger.Debug(\"did not match any distributions\")\n\t\t\tresp.Match = false\n\t\t\treturn resp, nil\n\t\t}\n\n\t\td := validDistributions[index]\n\t\ts.logger.Debug(\"matched distribution\", zap.Reflect(\"evaluation_distribution\", d))\n\n\t\tresp.Match = true\n\t\tresp.VariantKey = d.VariantKey\n\t\tresp.VariantAttachment = d.VariantAttachment\n\t\tresp.Reason = rpcevaluation.EvaluationReason_MATCH_EVALUATION_REASON\n\t\treturn resp, nil\n\t} // end rule loop\n\n\treturn resp, nil\n}\n\n// Boolean evaluates a request for a boolean flag and entity.\nfunc (s *Server) Boolean(ctx context.Context, r *rpcevaluation.EvaluationRequest) (*rpcevaluation.BooleanEvaluationResponse, resp, nil\n}\n\nfunc (s *Server) boolean(ctx context.Context, store storage.ReadOnlyStore, env environments.Environment, flag *core.Flag, r *rpcevaluation.EvaluationRequest) (*rpcevaluation.BooleanEvaluationResponse, error) {\n\trollouts, err := store.GetEvaluationRollouts(ctx, storage.NewResource(r.NamespaceKey, flag.Key, storage.WithReference(r.Reference)))\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\n\tvar (\n\t\tresp = &rpcevaluation.BooleanEvaluationResponse{\n\t\t\tRequestId: r.RequestId,\n\t\t}\n\t\tlastRank int32\n\t)\n\n\tvar (\n\t\tstartTime       = flagAttr)))\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tmetrics.EvaluationLatency.Record(\n\t\t\tctx,\n\t\t\tfloat64(time.Since(startTime).Nanoseconds())/1e6,\n\t\t\tmetric.WithAttributeSet(\n\t\t\t\tattribute.NewSet(\n\t\t\t\t\tenvironmentAttr,\n\t\t\t\t\tnamespaceAttr,\n\t\t\t\t\tflagAttr,\n\t\t\t\t),\n\t\t\t),\n\t\t)\n\t}()\n\n\tfor _, rollout := range rollouts {\n\t\tif rollout.Rank < lastRank {\n\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"rollout rank: %d detected out of order\", rollout.Rank)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tlastRank = rollout.Rank\n\n\t\tif rollout.Threshold != nil {\n\t\t\t// consistent hashing based on the entity id and flag key.\n\t\t\thash := crc32.ChecksumIEEE([]byte(r.EntityId + r.FlagKey))\n\n\t\t\tnormalizedValue := float32(int(hash) % 100)\n\n\t\t\t// if this case does not hold, fall through to the next rollout.\n\t\t\tif normalizedValue < rollout.Threshold.Percentage {\n\t\t\t\tresp.Enabled = rollout.Threshold.Value\n\t\t\t\tresp.Reason = rpcevaluation.EvaluationReason_MATCH_EVALUATION_REASON\n\t\t\t\tresp.FlagKey = flag.Key\n\t\t\t\ts.logger.Debug(\"threshold based matched\", zap.Int(\"rank\", int(rollout.Rank)), zap.String(\"rollout_type\", \"threshold\"))\n\t\t\t\treturn resp, nil\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t} else if rollout.Segment != nil {\n\n\t\t\tvar (\n\t\t\t\tsegmentMatches = 0\n\t\t\t\tsegmentKeys    = []string{}\n\t\t\t)\n\n\t\t\tfor k, v := range rollout.Segment.Segments {\n\t\t\t\tmatched, reason, err := s.matchConstraints(r.Context, v.Constraints, v.MatchType, r.EntityId)\n\t\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\treturn nil, err\n\t\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t\t// if we don't match the segment, fall through to the next rollout.\n\t\t\t\tif matched {\n\t\t\t\t\ts.logger.Debug(reason)\n\t\t\t\t\tsegmentKeys = append(segmentKeys, k)\n\t\t\t\t\tsegmentMatches++\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tswitch rollout.Segment.SegmentOperator {\n\t\t\tcase core.SegmentOperator_OR_SEGMENT_OPERATOR:\n\t\t\t\tif segmentMatches < 1 {\n\t\t\t\t\ts.logger.Debug(\"did not match ANY segments\")\n\t\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tcase core.SegmentOperator_AND_SEGMENT_OPERATOR:\n\t\t\t\tif len(rollout.Segment.Segments) != segmentMatches {\n\t\t\t\t\ts.logger.Debug(\"did not match ALL segments\")\n\t\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tresp.Enabled = rollout.Segment.Value\n\t\t\tresp.Reason = rpcevaluation.EvaluationReason_MATCH_EVALUATION_REASON\n\t\t\tresp.FlagKey = flag.Key\n\t\t\tresp.SegmentKeys = segmentKeys\n\n\t\t\ts.logger.Debug(\"segment based matched\", zap.Int(\"rank\", int(rollout.Rank)), zap.Strings(\"segments\", segmentKeys))\n\t\t\treturn resp, nil\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// If we have exhausted all rollouts and we still don't have a match, return flag enabled value.\n\tresp.Reason = rpcevaluation.EvaluationReason_DEFAULT_EVALUATION_REASON\n\tresp.Enabled = flag.Enabled\n\tresp.FlagKey = flag.Key\n\n\ts.logger.Debug(\"default rollout matched\", zap.Bool(\"enabled\", flag.Enabled))\n\treturn resp, nil\n}\n\n// Batch takes in a list of *evaluation.EvaluationRequest and returns their respective responses.\nfunc (s *Server) Batch(ctx context.Context, b *rpcevaluation.BatchEvaluationRequest) (*rpcevaluation.BatchEvaluationResponse, error) {\n\tresp := &rpcevaluation.BatchEvaluationResponse{\n\t\tResponses: make([]*rpcevaluation.EvaluationResponse, 0, len(b.Requests)),\n\t}\n\n\tfor _, req := range b.GetRequests() {\n\t\t// this is not ideal as it could lead to a lot of swapping the environment store if requests are coming in for different environments\n\t\t// we will need to document that while you CAN use different environments in the same request, it is not recommended and could have a performance impact\n\t\t// but since we are using an in-memory map it's probably not that bad\n\t\tenv, err := s.store.Get(ctx, req.EnvironmentKey)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t// try to get the environment from the context\n\t\t\t// this is for nil {\n\t\t\treturn nil, err\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tf, err := store.GetFlag(ctx, storage.NewResource(req.NamespaceKey, req.FlagKey, storage.WithReference(b.Reference)))\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\tvar errnf errs.ErrNotFound\n\t\t\tif errors.As(err, &errnf) {\n\t\t\t\teresp := &rpcevaluation.EvaluationResponse{\n\t\t\t\t\tType: rpcevaluation.EvaluationResponseType_ERROR_EVALUATION_RESPONSE_TYPE,\n\t\t\t\t\tResponse: &rpcevaluation.EvaluationResponse_ErrorResponse{\n\t\t\t\t\t\tErrorResponse: &rpcevaluation.ErrorEvaluationResponse{\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tFlagKey:      req.FlagKey,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tNamespaceKey: req.NamespaceKey,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tReason:       rpcevaluation.ErrorEvaluationReason_NOT_FOUND_ERROR_EVALUATION_REASON,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t},\n\t\t\t\t\t},\n\t\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t\tresp.Responses = append(resp.Responses, eresp)\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\treturn nil, err\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tswitch f.Type {\n\t\tcase core.FlagType_BOOLEAN_FLAG_TYPE:\n\t\t\tres, err := s.boolean(ctx, store, env, f, req)\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn nil, err\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tif s.tracingEnabled {\n\t\t\t\ts.addEvaluationEvent(ctx, env, req.NamespaceKey, req.FlagKey, req.EntityId, req.RequestId,\n\t\t\t\t\ttracing.AttributeVariant.Bool(res.Enabled),\n\t\t\t\t\ttracing.AttributeReason.String(tracing.ReasonToValue(res.Reason)),\n\t\t\t\t\ttracing.AttributeSegments.StringSlice(res.SegmentKeys),\n\t\t\t\t\ttracing.AttributeFlagTypeBoolean,\n\t\t\t\t)\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\teresp := &rpcevaluation.EvaluationResponse{\n\t\t\t\tType: rpcevaluation.EvaluationResponseType_BOOLEAN_EVALUATION_RESPONSE_TYPE,\n\t\t\t\tResponse: &rpcevaluation.EvaluationResponse_BooleanResponse{\n\t\t\t\t\tBooleanResponse: res,\n\t\t\t\t},\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tresp.Responses = append(resp.Responses, eresp)\n\t\tcase core.FlagType_VARIANT_FLAG_TYPE:\n\t\t\tres, err := s.variant(ctx, store, env, f, req)\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn nil, err\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tif s.tracingEnabled {\n\t\t\t\ts.addEvaluationEvent(ctx, env, req.NamespaceKey, req.FlagKey, req.EntityId, req.RequestId,\n\t\t\t\t\ttracing.AttributeMatch.Bool(res.Match),\n\t\t\t\t\ttracing.AttributeVariant.String(res.VariantKey),\n\t\t\t\t\ttracing.AttributeReason.String(tracing.ReasonToValue(res.Reason)),\n\t\t\t\t\ttracing.AttributeSegments.StringSlice(res.SegmentKeys),\n\t\t\t\t\ttracing.AttributeFlagTypeVariant,\n\t\t\t\t)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\teresp := &rpcevaluation.EvaluationResponse{\n\t\t\t\tType: rpcevaluation.EvaluationResponseType_VARIANT_EVALUATION_RESPONSE_TYPE,\n\t\t\t\tResponse: &rpcevaluation.EvaluationResponse_VariantResponse{\n\t\t\t\t\tVariantResponse: res,\n\t\t\t\t},\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tresp.Responses = append(resp.Responses, eresp)\n\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\treturn nil, errs.ErrInvalidf(\"unknown flag type: %s\", f.Type)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn resp, nil\n}\n\n// matchConstraints is a utility function that will return if all or any constraints have matched for a segment depending\n// on the match type.\nfunc (s *Server) matchConstraints(evalCtx map[string]string, constraints []storage.EvaluationConstraint, segmentMatchType core.MatchType, entityId string) (bool, string, error) {\n\tconstraintMatches := 0\n\n\tvar reason string\n\n\tfor _, c := range constraints {\n\t\tv := evalCtx[c.Property]\n\n\t\tvar (\n\t\t\tmatch bool\n\t\t\terr   error\n\t\t)\n\n\t\tswitch c.Type {\n\t\tcase core.ComparisonType_STRING_COMPARISON_TYPE:\n\t\t\tmatch = matchesString(c, v)\n\t\tcase core.ComparisonType_NUMBER_COMPARISON_TYPE:\n\t\t\tmatch, err = matchesNumber(c, v)\n\t\tcase core.ComparisonType_BOOLEAN_COMPARISON_TYPE:\n\t\t\tmatch, err = matchesBool(c, v)\n\t\tcase core.ComparisonType_DATETIME_COMPARISON_TYPE:\n\t\t\tmatch, err = match all constraints\n\t\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\t\t// keep looping to see if we match the next constraint\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tmatched := true\n\n\tswitch core.MatchType_ANY_MATCH_TYPE:\n\t\tif len(constraints) > 0 && constraintMatches == 0 {\n\t\t\treason = \"did not match ANY constraints\"\n\t\t\tmatched = false\n\t\t}\n\tdefault:\n\t\treason = fmt.Sprintf(\"unknown match type %d\", segmentMatchType)\n\t\tmatched = false\n\t}\n\n\treturn matched, reason, nil\n}\n\nfunc crc32Num(entityID string, salt string) uint {\n\treturn 100\n)\n\nfunc matchesString(c storage.EvaluationConstraint, v string) bool {\n\tswitch c.Operator {\n\tcase flipt.OpEmpty:\n\t\treturn len(strings.TrimSpace(v)) == 0\n\tcase append(dt.durations, d)\n}\n\n// Count returns the total number of recorded evaluations.\nfunc (dt *DurationTracker) Count() int {\n\tdt.mu.RLock()\n\tdefer dt.mu.RUnlock()\n\treturn len(dt.durations)\n}\n\n// Average returns the average duration across all recorded evaluations.\n// Returns 0 if no durations have been recorded.\nfunc (dt *DurationTracker) Average() time.Duration {\n\tdt.mu.RLock()\n\tdefer dt.mu.RUnlock()\n\n\tif len(dt.durations) == 0 {\n\t\treturn 0\n\t}\n\n\tvar total time.Duration\n\tfor _, d := range dt.durations {\n\t\ttotal += d\n\t}\n\n\treturn total / time.Duration(len(dt.durations))\n}\n\n// P99 returns the 99th percentile duration.\n// Returns 0 if no durations have been recorded.\nfunc (dt *DurationTracker) P99() time.Duration {\n\tdt.mu.RLock()\n\tdefer dt.mu.RUnlock()\n\n\tif len(dt.durations) == 0 {\n\t\treturn 0\n\t}\n\n\t// Create a sorted copy of durations\n\tsorted := make([]time.Duration, 2. WRITE /workspace/internal/server/evaluation/server.go
package evaluation

import (
	"context"

	"go.flipt.io/flipt/internal/storage"
	"go.flipt.io/flipt/rpc/flipt"
	"go.flipt.io/flipt/rpc/flipt/evaluation"
	"go.uber.org/zap"
	"google.golang.org/grpc"
)

// Storer is the minimal abstraction for interacting with the storage layer for evaluation.
type Storer interface {
	GetFlag(ctx context.Context, flag storage.ResourceRequest) (*flipt.Flag, error)
	GetEvaluationRules(ctx context.Context, flag storage.ResourceRequest) ([]*storage.EvaluationRule, error)
	GetEvaluationDistributions(ctx context.Context, ruleID storage.IDRequest) ([]*storage.EvaluationDistribution, error)
	GetEvaluationRollouts(ctx context.Context, flag storage.ResourceRequest) ([]*storage.EvaluationRollout, error)
}

// Server serves the Flipt evaluate v2 gRPC Server.
type Server struct {
	logger            *zap.Logger
	store             Storer
	evaluator         *Evaluator
	durationTracker   *DurationTracker
	evaluation.UnimplementedEvaluationServiceServer
}

// New is constructs a new Server.
func New(logger *zap.Logger, store Storer) *Server {
	return &Server{
		logger:          logger,
		store:           store,
		evaluator:       NewEvaluator(logger, store),
		durationTracker: NewDurationTracker(),
	}
}

// RegisterGRPC registers the EvaluateServer onto the provided gRPC Server.
func (s *Server) RegisterGRPC(server *grpc.Server) {
	evaluation.RegisterEvaluationServiceServer(server, s)
}

func (s *Server) AllowsNamespaceScopedAuthentication(ctx context.Context) bool {
	return true
}

3. WRITE /workspace/internal/server/evaluation/duration_tracker.go
package evaluation

import (
	"sort"
	"sync"
	"time"
)

// DurationTracker records evaluation durations and provides aggregate statistics
// in a thread-safe manner.
type DurationTracker struct {
	mu        sync.RWMutex
	durations []time.Duration
}

// NewDurationTracker creates a new DurationTracker.
func NewDurationTracker() *DurationTracker {
	return &DurationTracker{
		durations: make([]time.Duration, 0),
	}
}

// Record records a duration for an evaluation.
func (dt *DurationTracker) Record(d time.Duration) {
	dt.mu.Lock()
	defer dt.mu.Unlock()
	dt.durations = append(dt.durations, d)
}

// Count returns the total number of recorded evaluations.
func (dt *DurationTracker) Count() int {
	dt.mu.RLock()
	defer dt.mu.RUnlock()
	return len(dt.durations)
}

// Average returns the average duration across all recorded evaluations.
// Returns 0 if no durations have been recorded.
func (dt *DurationTracker) Average() time.Duration {
	dt.mu.RLock()
	defer dt.mu.RUnlock()

	if len(dt.durations) == 0 {
		return 0
	}

	var total time.Duration
	for _, d := range dt.durations {
		total += d
	}

	return total / time.Duration(len(dt.durations))
}

// P99 returns the 99th percentile duration.
// Returns 0 if no durations have been recorded.
func (dt *DurationTracker) P99() time.Duration {
	dt.mu.RLock()
	defer dt.mu.RUnlock()

	if len(dt.durations) == 0 {
		return 0
	}

	// Create a sorted copy of durations
	sorted := make([]time.Duration, len(dt.durations))
	copy(sorted, dt.durations)
	sort.Slice(sorted, func(i, j int) bool {
		return sorted[i] < sorted[j]
	})

	// Calculate the index for the 99th percentile
	// Using linear interpolation method
	index := int(float64(len(sorted)-1) * 0.99)
	if index >= len(sorted) {
		index = len(sorted) - 1
	}

	return sorted[index]
}

// Variant evaluates a request for a multi-variate flag and entity.
// It adapts the 'v2' evaluation API and proxies the request to the 'v1' evaluation API.
func (s *Server) Variant(ctx context.Context, r *rpcevaluation.EvaluationRequest) (*rpcevaluation.VariantEvaluationResponse, error) {
	startTime := time.Now()
	defer func() {
		s.durationTracker.Record(time.Since(startTime))
	}()

	flag, err := s.store.GetFlag(ctx, storage.NewResource(r.NamespaceKey, r.FlagKey, storage.WithReference(r.Reference)))
	if err != nil {
		return nil, err
	}

	s.logger.Debug("variant", zap.Stringer("request", r))

	resp, err := s.variant(ctx, flag, r)
	if err != nil {
		return nil, err
	}

	spanAttrs := []attribute.KeyValue{
		fliptotel.AttributeNamespace.String(r.NamespaceKey),
		fliptotel.AttributeFlag.String(r.FlagKey),
		fliptotel.AttributeEntityID.String(r.EntityId),
		fliptotel.AttributeRequestID.String(r.RequestId),
		fliptotel.AttributeMatch.Bool(resp.Match),
		fliptotel.AttributeValue.String(resp.VariantKey),
		fliptotel.AttributeReason.String(resp.Reason.String()),
		fliptotel.AttributeSegments.StringSlice(resp.SegmentKeys),
		fliptotel.AttributeFlagKey(resp.FlagKey),
		fliptotel.AttributeProviderName,
		fliptotel.AttributeFlagVariant(resp.VariantKey),
	}

	// add otel attributes to span
	span := trace.SpanFromCon

// Server serves the Flipt evaluate v2 gRPC Server.
type Server struct {
	logger            *zap.Logger
	store             EnvironmentStore
	tracingEnabled    bool
	durationTracker   *DurationTracker
	evaluation.UnimplementedEvaluationServiceServer
}

// New is constructs a new Server.
func New(logger *zap.Logger, store EnvironmentStore, ops ...Option) *Server {
	s := &Server{
		logger: logger,
		store:  store,
	}

	for _, o := range ops {
		o(s)
	}

	return s
}
After
// New is constructs a new Server.
func New(logger *zap.Logger, store EnvironmentStore, ops ...Option) *Server {
	s := &Server{
		logger:          logger,
		store:           store,
		durationTracker: NewDurationTracker(),
	}

	for _, o := range ops {
		o(s)
	}

	return s
}
13. EDIT /workspace/internal/server/evaluation/evaluation.go
Before
// Variant evaluates a request for a multi-variate flag and entity.
func (s *Server) Variant(ctx context.Context, r *rpcevaluation.EvaluationRequest) (*rpcevaluation.VariantEvaluationResponse, error) {
	env, err := s.store.Get(ctx, r.EnvironmentKey)
	if err != nil {
		// try to get the environment from the context
		// this is for backwards compatibility with v1
		env, err = s.store.GetFromContext(ctx)
		if err != nil {
			return nil, err
		}
	}

	store, err := env.EvaluationStore()
	if err != nil {
		return nil, err
	}

	flag, err := store.GetFlag(ctx, storage.NewResource(r.NamespaceKey, r.FlagKey, storage.WithReference(r.Reference)))
	if err != nil {
		return nil, err
	}

	if flag.Type != core.FlagType_VARIANT_FLAG_TYPE {
		return nil, errs.ErrInvalidf("flag type %s invalid", flag.Type)
	}

	resp, err := s.variant(ctx, store, env, flag, r)
	if err != nil {
		return nil, err
	}

	if s.tracingEnabled {
		s.addEvaluationEvent(ctx, env, r.NamespaceKey, r.FlagKey, r.EntityId, r.RequestId,
			tracing.AttributeMatch.Bool(resp.Match),
			tracing.AttributeVariant.String(resp.VariantKey),
			tracing.AttributeReason.String(tracing.ReasonToValue(resp.Reason)),
			tracing.AttributeSegments.StringSlice(resp.SegmentKeys),
			tracing.AttributeFlagTypeVariant,
		)
	}

	return resp, nil
}
After
// Variant evaluates a request for a multi-variate flag and entity.
func (s *Server) Variant(ctx context.Context, r *rpcevaluation.EvaluationRequest) (*rpcevaluation.VariantEvaluationResponse, error) {
	startTime := time.Now()
	defer func() {
		s.durationTracker.Record(time.Since(startTime))
	}()

	env, err := s.store.Get(ctx, r.EnvironmentKey)
	if err != nil {
		// try to get the environment from the context
		// this is for backwards compatibility with v1
		env, err = s.store.GetFromContext(ctx)
		if err != nil {
			return nil, err
		}
	}

	store, err := env.EvaluationStore()
	if err != nil {
		return nil, err
	}

	flag, err := store.GetFlag(ctx, storage.NewResource(r.NamespaceKey, r.FlagKey, storage.WithReference(r.Reference)))
	if err != nil {
		return nil, err
	}

	if flag.Type != core.FlagType_VARIANT_FLAG_TYPE {
		return nil, errs.ErrInvalidf("flag type %s invalid", flag.Type)
	}

	resp, err := s.variant(ctx, store, env, flag, r)
	if err != nil {
		return nil, err
	}

	if s.tracingEnabled {
		s.addEvaluationEvent(ctx, env, r.NamespaceKey, r.FlagKey, r.EntityId, r.RequestId,
			tracing.AttributeMatch.Bool(resp.Match),
			tracing.AttributeVariant.String(resp.VariantKey),
			tracing.AttributeReason.String(tracing.ReasonToValue(resp.Reason)),
			tracing.AttributeSegments.StringSlice(resp.SegmentKeys),
			tracing.AttributeFlagTypeVariant,
		)
	}

	return resp, nil
}

// Boolean evaluates a request for a boolean flag and entity.
func (s *Server) Boolean(ctx context.Context, r *rpcevaluation.EvaluationRequest) (*rpcevaluation.BooleanEvaluationResponse, error) {
	startTime := time.Now()
	defer func() {
		s.durationTracker.Record(time.Since(startTime))
	}()

	env, err := s.store.Get(ctx, r.EnvironmentKey)
	if err != nil {
		// try to get the environment from the context
		// this is for backwards compatibility with v1
		env, err = s.store.GetFromContext(ctx)
		if err != nil {
			return nil, err
		}
	}

	store, err := env.EvaluationStore()
	if err != nil {
		return nil, err
	}

	flag, err := store.GetFlag(ctx, storage.NewResource(r.NamespaceKey, r.FlagKey, storage.WithReference(r.Reference)))
	if err != nil {
		return nil, err
	}

	if flag.Type != core.FlagType_BOOLEAN_FLAG_TYPE {
		return nil, errs.ErrInvalidf("flag type %s invalid", flag.Type)
	}

	resp, err := s.boolean(ctx, store, env, flag, r)
	if err != nil {
		return nil, err
	}

	if s.tracingEnabled {
		s.addEvaluationEvent(ctx, env, r.NamespaceKey, r.FlagKey, r.EntityId, r.RequestId,
			tracing.AttributeVariant.Bool(resp.Enabled),
			tracing.AttributeReason.String(tracing.ReasonToValue(resp.Reason)),
			tracing.AttributeSegments.StringSlice(resp.SegmentKeys),
			tracing.AttributeFlagTypeBoolean,
		)
	}

	return resp, nil
}

cat > duration_tracker.go << 'EOF'
package main

import (
	"sort"
	"sync"
	"time"
)

// DurationTracker records evaluation durations and provides aggregate statistics
// in a thread-safe manner.
type DurationTracker struct {
	mu        sync.RWMutex
	durations []time.Duration
}

// NewDurationTracker creates a new DurationTracker.
func NewDurationTracker() *DurationTracker {
	return &DurationTracker{
		durations: make([]time.Duration, 0),
	}
}

// Record records a duration for an evaluation.
func (dt *DurationTracker) Record(d time.Duration) {
	dt.mu.Lock()
	defer dt.mu.Unlock()
	dt.durations = append(dt.durations, d)
}

// Count returns the total number of recorded evaluations.
func (dt *DurationTracker) Count() int {
	dt.mu.RLock()
	defer dt.mu.RUnlock()
	return len(dt.durations)
}

// Average returns the average duration across all recorded evaluations.
// Returns 0 if no durations have been recorded.
func (dt *DurationTracker) Average() time.Duration {
	dt.mu.RLock()
	defer dt.mu.RUnlock()

	if len(dt.durations) == 0 {
		return 0
	}

	var total time.Duration
	for _, d := range dt.durations {
		total += d
	}

	return total / time.Duration(len(dt.durations))
}

// P99 returns the 99th percentile duration.
// Returns 0 if no durations have been recorded.
func (dt *DurationTracker) P99() time.Duration {
	dt.mu.RLock()
	defer dt.mu.RUnlock()

	if len(dt.durations) == 0 {
		return 0
	}

	// Create a sorted copy of durations
	sorted := make([]time.Duration, len(dt.durations))
	copy(sorted, dt.durations)
	sort.Slice(sorted, func(i, j int) bool {
		return sorted[i] < sorted[j]
	})

	// Calculate the index for the 99th percentile
	// Using linear interpolation method
	index := int(float64(len(sorted)-1) * 0.99)
	if index >= len(sorted) {
		index = len(sorted) - 1
	}

	return sorted[index]
}

func main() {}
EOF
go build . 2>&1

18. $ cd /tmp/test_duration && cat > test.go << 'EOF'
package main

import (
	"fmt"
	"time"
)

func TestDurationTracker() {
	dt := NewDurationTracker()
	
	// Record some durations
	dt.Record(100 * time.Millisecond)
	dt.Record(200 * time.Millisecond)
	dt.Record(150 * time.Millisecond)
	dt.Record(500 * time.Millisecond)
	dt.Record(75 * time.Millisecond)
	
	fmt.Printf("Count: %d\n", dt.Count())
	fmt.Printf("Average: %v\n", dt.Average())
	fmt.Printf("P99: %v\n", dt.P99())
	
	// Verify expected behavior
	if dt.Count() != 5 {
		panic("Count should be 5")
	}
	
	// Average should be approximately 205ms
	avg := dt.Average()
	if avg < 200*time.Millisecond || avg > 210*time.Millisecond {
		fmt.Printf("WARNING: Average seems off: %v\n", avg)
	}
	
	// P99 should be one of the higher values
	p99 := dt.P99()
	if p99 < 150*time.Millisecond {
		panic("P99 should be high")
	}
	
	fmt.Println("✓ All tests passed")
}

func main() {
	TestDurationTracker()
}
EOF
go run . && echo "✓ Duration tracker test successful"

package main

import (
	"sort"
	"sync"
	"time"
)

// DurationTracker records evaluation durations and provides aggregate statistics
// in a thread-safe manner.
type DurationTracker struct {
	mu        sync.RWMutex
	durations []time.Duration
}

// NewDurationTracker creates a new DurationTracker.
func NewDurationTracker() *DurationTracker {
	return &DurationTracker{
		durations: make([]time.Duration, 0),
	}
}

// Record records a duration for an evaluation.
func (dt *DurationTracker) Record(d time.Duration) {
	dt.mu.Lock()
	defer dt.mu.Unlock()
	dt.durations = append(dt.durations, d)
}

// Count returns the total number of recorded evaluations.
func (dt *DurationTracker) Count() int {
	dt.mu.RLock()
	defer dt.mu.RUnlock()
	return len(dt.durations)
}

// Average returns the average duration across all recorded evaluations.
// Returns 0 if no durations have been recorded.
func (dt *DurationTracker) Average() time.Duration {
	dt.mu.RLock()
	defer dt.mu.RUnlock()

	if len(dt.durations) == 0 {
		return 0
	}

	var total time.Duration
	for _, d := range dt.durations {
		total += d
	}

	return total / time.Duration(len(dt.durations))
}

// P99 returns the 99th percentile duration.
// Returns 0 if no durations have been recorded.
func (dt *DurationTracker) P99() time.Duration {
	dt.mu.RLock()
	defer dt.mu.RUnlock()

	if len(dt.durations) == 0 {
		return 0
	}

	// Create a sorted copy of durations
	sorted := make([]time.Duration, len(dt.durations))
	copy(sorted, dt.durations)
	sort.Slice(sorted, func(i, j int) bool {
		return sorted[i] < sorted[j]
	})

	// Calculate the index for the 99th percentile
	// Using linear interpolation method
	index := int(float64(len(sorted)-1) * 0.99)
	if index >= len(sorted) {
		index = len(sorted) - 1
	}

	return sorted[index]
}
EOF
